<P id=pfc27e739-f7bf-43bb-87a6-4bddbc9b913a style="MARGIN: 0px"><B>Section 3 &#8211; Securities and Trading Markets.</B></P>
<P id=p8a4b0df2-ae85-45f5-b6c2-9383f3484951 style="MARGIN: 0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P id=p26f144ad-536c-4c00-b700-25a8228898b3 style="MARGIN: 0px"><B>Item 3.02 Unregistered Sales of Equity Securities.</B></P>
<P id=pdc6e5712-5e74-4496-8066-330c20749e76 style="MARGIN: 0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P id=pd8df0b2c-69c5-4401-8549-8dee8b516848 style="MARGIN: 0px"><I>JMJ Financial</I></P>
<P id=pdc486bdb-fa92-4efb-84b3-8d252f502bbd style="MARGIN: 0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P id=p63d0ea26-95af-446b-9037-9aa526abd795 style="MARGIN: 0px; TEXT-INDENT: 45px">On July 20, 2015, we issued a $200,000 Convertible Note (the "Note") to JMJ Financial. The Note contains a ten percent (10%) original issue discount, and is to be funded in tranches at the sole discretion of JMJ. The first tranche was for $20,000. The Note has a maturity date of two years from the funding of each tranche and is convertible at the lesser of $0.02 or 60% of the lowest trade price in the 25 trading days before conversion. Each tranche is subject to a one-time interest charge of 12% 90 days after its funding. The Note can be prepaid by us only during the first 90 days following the issuance of each funding tranche. The purchase and sale of the Note closed on July 23, 2015, the date that the purchase price was delivered to us.</P>
<P id=p98b562ba-fc75-4c73-b436-42e6b9558e34 style="MARGIN: 0px; TEXT-INDENT: 45px"></P>
<P id=pb6d26440-96e6-4355-8fca-8b03612ad7d5 style="MARGIN: 0px; TEXT-INDENT: 45px">&nbsp;</P>
<P id=p15200426-957d-486a-81fb-3a36dcc18a44 style="MARGIN: 0px; TEXT-INDENT: 45px">&nbsp;The issuance of the Note was exempt from the registration requirements under the Securities Act of 1933 pursuant to Section 4(a)(2) thereof. The purchaser was an accredited and sophisticated investor, familiar with our operations, and there was no solicitation.</P>
<P id=p3da1d9b4-6fdd-4499-8550-ef7b8ab935ca style="MARGIN: 0px">&nbsp;</P>
